msg:This is the "first city in the extreme" written by Xu Xiake, and it is the most remote place he has ever visited in his life. Welcome to Tengchong, a small border town located at the foot of the volcano.

"The rainy season in Yunnan,
More than just a solar term,
It represents the Yunnan-Guizhou Plateau where all things grow.
Miracles are happening. "

The first stop to meet Tengchong started from the "Linghe Crossing" on a rainy day.
Books always like to write about overjoyed evenings.
In my eyes, this most ordinary evening,
Because the scenery in front of me has a different color.

What we thought was a surprise encounter,
Who knows how much careful polishing it has gone through?
There is always a reason for every encounter in life,
On a sleepless night in Mangshi,
I saw the mountains and forests in Tengchong through someone elseâ€™s lens.
So a certain part of us,
There must be something the same.

Just like the distant mountains seen halfway up the mountain, the dense mist after the night rain, the surprise in the eyes of the century-old trees, the mellow aroma of the flower cakes baked by the hotel sister, and the comfortable bathrobe that fills the nostrils , hot milk before going to bed, the comfort of stone pool hot springs, the rush of green fields in the morning, the chirping of birds, and my favorite soft toothbrush, all tell me that these are the same places for us.

If you come here not only for the beautiful scenery of the mountains and fields, but also for a good night's sleep while "listening to the lotus crossing". Unfortunately, the "Linghe Ferry" from Tengchong cannot be carried back to Shanghai. Fortunately, I can take away the two pillows that let me sleep deeply and freely.

I prefer any place that makes me relax physically and mentally. I canâ€™t refuse to be impressed by all the carefully prepared details, such as infinity swimming pool, gym, small garden with lawn, open-air movie, and making tea by the fire. We might as well be bold and go where we want to go. place, itâ€™s never too late.

Maybe this is what made me decide to transfer to Tengchong on a whim. Tengchong is beautiful and the hotel is very good. I will come again next time.

msg:I also stayed in a hotel that I liked in Tengchong. Linghedu Banshan simply met all my requirements for a top hotel.
Environment:
The lobby of the hotel extends out to a large viewing platform. The terrace integrates the sky and the mountains and waters. Here you can see the beautiful sunset of Tengchong, like a beautiful landscape painting.
There are beautiful arched flower corridors, large rocking chairs and swings, and camping tents and tables and chairs in the garden, which can be brought to the hotel for a whole day.

Facilities:
The soft and hard decoration, bathroom facilities, and bedding supplies in the room are all very good brands, with full quality and details. There is a large hot spring bath on the balcony of the room, and there are hot spring bath lights in the hot spring! In addition, the hotel also has an infinity pool and a gym, which simply provides guests with all the facilities that can be provided. It can be seen that the boss is a person who has extremely high requirements for taste, quality and experience, and even has a bit of craftsmanship. Otherwise, how can he create such a perfect and impeccable work.

Service:
Before checking in, the housekeeper will contact whether you need to pick up and drop off. Any WeChat messages to the housekeeper sister will be replied as soon as possible. The first thing to do after arriving at the hotel is not to check in, but to invite you to drink tea, eat some fruits and flower cakes, eat well, drink well and rest well before checking in. I have stayed in so many five-star hotels in China, and this is the first time I have experienced such a caring check-in experience. I can feel the hard work and sincerity of the boss and the integrated operation team.

Breakfast:
Outside the glass window of the restaurant is an open terrace, facing the mountains and the morning sun for breakfast. The breakfast is a set meal, exquisite and delicious.

It is really a very good experience. Next time I come to Tengchong, I will choose Linghedu~

It is said that there is no life without mistakes, but in the right place, mistakes seem to be slowly corrected, and Linghedu is such a place.

I like its reception platform very much. It has a surreal artistic conception of Dali's "Columbus Dream". When the sun is good, standing in front of the French window, Tengchong has a panoramic view, and the water and sky are reflected in the shadows. Slowly closing your eyes will trigger various subconscious and eliminate mental crises.

There is a Great Dane here, 9 years old, named BajieğŸ·. The proprietress said that Bajie came when he was more than 3 months old. My girlfriend leaned lightly on Bajie, and it shook reflexively and continued to rest.

Sometimes people can't communicate with each other. Bajie is very calm. I think he can understand it. The older I get, the lonelier I get. Bajie thinks that the various aspects of the world are no longer worth laughing at. It dropped its head into the sun, as if to say, today's sun can't shine on tomorrow's clothes. Now that you're here, enjoy Linghedu.

Yes, today's umbrella can't cover tomorrow's rain. We soaked in the hot spring water and saw the sun, drizzle, and quiet night. With a bun on our heads, cigars and wine are a natural match! Time in Linghedu is like hot spring water, bringing people and things, and taking them away together.

I won't go into details about the soft furnishings and conditions in the room. The boss has considered it very carefully, from the temperature to the toilet, enough to keep the guests. There is a painting collection in the room: freehand Zen, there is Zen in the painting, it doesn't deliberately guide, but it illuminates the way forward, it's worth tasting.

Linghedu is just like this album, it's worth tasting in detail, the ink splashing and the blank space are just right, the silent service is everywhere, not delicate, not deliberate.

We also booked a travel photography here, which is also one of the characteristics of Linghedu. The photos are amazing. I recommend you give it a try!
